WHERE ((NOT (`p`.`IsDeleted`) AND (`p`.`CompanyId` = @ef_filter__CurrentCompanyId)) AND NOT (`p`.`IsDeleted`)) AND (`p`.`Year` = @request_Year_Value)

SELECT `p`.`Id`, `p`.`AmountPaid`, `p`.`CompanyId`, `p`.`CreatedBy`, `p`.`CreatedDate`, `p`.`DeletedBy`, `p`.`DeletedDate`, `p`.`ExpectedDeliveryDate`, `p`.`IsDeleted`, `p`.`ModifiedBy`, `p`.`ModifiedDate`, `p`.`Notes`, `p`.`OrderCode`, `p`.`OrderDate`, `p`.`Status`, `p`.`SupplierId`, `p`.`TotalAmount`, `s0`.`Id`, `s0`.`Address`, `s0`.`BankAccountNumber`, `s0`.`BankName`, `s0`.`CompanyId`, `s0`.`CreatedBy`, `s0`.`CreatedDate`, `s0`.`DeletedBy`, `s0`.`DeletedDate`, `s0`.`Email`, `s0`.`FullName`, `s0`.`IsDeleted`, `s0`.`ModifiedBy`, `s0`.`ModifiedDate`, `s0`.`Notes`, `s0`.`PhoneNumber`
FROM `PurchaseOrders` AS `p`
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT `s`.`Id`, `s`.`Address`, `s`.`BankAccountNumber`, `s`.`BankName`, `s`.`CompanyId`, `s`.`CreatedBy`, `s`.`CreatedDate`, `s`.`DeletedBy`, `s`.`DeletedDate`, `s`.`Email`, `s`.`FullName`, `s`.`IsDeleted`, `s`.`ModifiedBy`, `s`.`ModifiedDate`, `s`.`Notes`, `s`.`PhoneNumber`
    FROM `Suppliers` AS `s`
    WHERE NOT (`s`.`IsDeleted`) AND (`s`.`CompanyId` = @ef_filter__CurrentCompanyId)
) AS `s0` ON `p`.`SupplierId` = `s0`.`Id`
WHERE NOT (`p`.`IsDeleted`) AND (`p`.`CompanyId` = @ef_filter__CurrentCompanyId)
ORDER BY `p`.`OrderDate` DESC

    WHERE NOT (`s`.`IsDeleted`) AND (`s`.`CompanyId` = @ef_filter__CurrentCompanyId)
) AS `s0` ON `p`.`SupplierId` = `s0`.`Id`
WHERE NOT (`p`.`IsDeleted`) AND (`p`.`CompanyId` = @ef_filter__CurrentCompanyId)
ORDER BY `p`.`OrderDate` DESC
